// Modified Table (contains all custom objects)

@compiletime function create_w3u_h000()
	let def = createObjectDefinition("w3u", 'h000', 'hpea')
	..setReal("usca", 0.5)
	..setString("utub", "The |cffff8000Peasant |rmight not get much recognition for his work though it is nonetheless a vital and perhaps even the most important part when trying to raise a Kingdom.|n|n|cffffcc00Builds basic structures, can also harvest resources.|r")
	..setInt("usin", 400)
	..setUnreal("uacq", 250.0)
	..setInt("ua1r", 42)
	..setInt("ua2r", 50)
	..setInt("umvs", 128)
	..setUnreal("urb1", 138.0)
	..setReal("ussc", 0.5)
	..setReal("ushx", 20.0)
	..setReal("ushy", 20.0)
	..setReal("ushh", 50.0)
	..setReal("ushw", 50.0)
	..setUnreal("uimz", 30.0)
	..setString("ubui", "h00M,h00Y,h008,h007,h010,h011,h015,h009,h00X,h013,h014,h00Q")
	..setUnreal("ucol", 12.0)
	..setString("uabi", "A03P,Ahar,Ahrp,A02A")
	..setString("utip", "Train Peasant (|cffff0000Q|r)")
	..setString("uhot", "Q")
	..setInt("ua1s", 1)
	..setUnreal("uhpr", 0.0)
	..setInt("ubld", 7)
	..setString("unam", "Peasant ")
	..setInt("uhpm", 250)
	..setInt("ulev", 0)
	..setInt("ugol", 6)
	..setInt("usid", 400)
	..setString("udty", "none")
